	available = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_RFK_CONTELPRO_Currently_Investigating }
	}
	visible = {
		has_country_flag = USA_RFK_CONTELPRO_Active
		has_country_flag = USA_RFK_CONTELPRO_Southerners_Activated
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	cost = 40
	days_remove = 25

	complete_effect = {
		set_country_flag = USA_RFK_CONTELPRO_Currently_Investigating
	}

	remove_effect = {
		clr_country_flag = USA_RFK_CONTELPRO_Currently_Investigating
		set_country_flag = USA_RFK_NPPFR_Investigation_Available
		country_event = { id = bobby.contelpro.1 days = 3 }
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_country_flag = BRG_dissent_within_flag
		}
	}
}

USA_black_market_category = {
	USA_sell_arms = {
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_black_market
		}
		#you have to ship the most recent guns
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = USA_has_arms_shipment_tooltip
				USA_has_arms_shipment = yes
			}
		}
		days_remove = 5
		days_re_enable = 180
		cost = 25
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_sell_arms"
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = USA_recent_sale
				days = 90
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = -1000
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = anti_tank_equipment
				amount = -400
			}
			}
	}

	USA_radio_free_england = {
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_black_market
			has_completed_focus = USA_mother_britannia_needs_us
		}
		available = {
			has_country_flag = USA_black_market
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_radio_free_england"

		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove USA_radio_free_england"
			add_to_variable = { rebellion = 5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = Rebellion_minor
		}
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.05
		}
		days_remove = 60
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 100
	}

	USA_supplementary_shipments_ENG = {
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_black_market
			has_completed_focus = USA_mother_britannia_needs_us
		}
		available = {

		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_supplementary_shipments_ENG"

				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = -1500
				producer = USA
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = anti_tank_equipment
				amount = -600
				producer = USA
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove USA_supplementary_shipments_ENG"
			add_to_variable = { rebellion = 5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = Rebellion_minor
		}
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.05
		}

	}

USA_draft_mobilization_category = {
	USA_no_war_demobilize = {
		allowed = { tag = USA }
		available = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = tno_conscription_volunteer_only
				has_idea = tno_conscription_disarmed_nation
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_mobilized_national_guard }
		}
		activation = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { USA_policing_variable > 0 }
					check_variable = { USA_advisor_variable > 0 }
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_idea = tno_conscription_one_year_draft
				has_idea = tno_conscription_two_year_draft
				has_idea = tno_conscription_four_year_draft
				has_country_flag = USA_mobilized_national_guard
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 90
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout USA_no_war_demobilize"
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.10
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = tno_conscription_one_year_draft }
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = tno_conscription_volunteer_only
					remove_idea = tno_conscription_one_year_draft
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = tno_conscription_two_year_draft }
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = tno_conscription_volunteer_only
					remove_idea = tno_conscription_two_year_draft
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = tno_conscription_four_year_draft }
				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = tno_conscription_volunteer_only
					remove_idea = tno_conscription_four_year_draft
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_mobilized_national_guard }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "National Guard Infantry Division"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "National Guard Armored Division"
				}
				hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = USA_mobilized_national_guard }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_no_war_demobilize"
			#Your country doesn't explode, or something
		}

USA_LBJ_great_society_category = {
	#The NPP center's demands for civil rights from LBJ if he makes a deal with them
	USA_LBJ_NPP_C_pressure = {
		allowed = { tag = USA }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = USA_LBJ_completed_NPP_C_demands
				NOT = { has_variable = LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
		activation = {
			has_variable = LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 90
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout USA_LBJ_NPP_C_pressure"
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand = 0 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_LBJ_increase_NPP_demand_urgency_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_strengthen_center
				add_political_power = -50
				hidden_effect = {
					every_owned_state = { #They steal voters from you
						limit = {
							can_have_elections_in_state = yes
							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
								check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
								check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
							}
						}
						set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand = 1 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_LBJ_increase_NPP_demand_urgency_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_strengthen_center
				add_political_power = -50
				hidden_effect = {
					every_owned_state = { #They steal voters from you
						limit = {
							can_have_elections_in_state = yes
							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
								check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
								check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
							}
						}
						set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand = 2 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_LBJ_increase_NPP_demand_urgency_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_strengthen_center
				add_political_power = -50
				hidden_effect = {
					every_owned_state = { #They steal voters from you
						limit = {
							can_have_elections_in_state = yes
							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
								check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
								check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
							}
						}
						set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.06 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand = 3 } }
				add_political_power = -100
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_LBJ_NPP_demand_break_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_strengthen_center
				hidden_effect = {
					every_owned_state = { #They steal voters from you
						limit = {
							can_have_elections_in_state = yes
							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
								check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
								check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
							}
						}
						set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.07 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					}
					clr_country_flag = USA_R_Center_United
					clear_variable = LBJ_NPP_civil_rights_demand
				}
			}

						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
							check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
							check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
						}

					subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.04 }

	USA_LBJ_crack_down_southern_businesses = {
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = USA_lbj_64_once_more_unto_the_breach
			tag = USA
		}
		available = { tag = USA }
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 40
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_LBJ_crack_down_southern_businesses"
			USA_lbj_strengthen_civil_rights_small = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_anger_south
			TNO_improve_poverty_low = yes
			set_country_flag = LBJ_crack_down_businesses_flag
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
						NOT = { check_variable = { nationality = 337 } } #Unchannging Corn
					}
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.01 }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 84 } } #African American
						add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.03 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
								check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
								check_variable = { nationality = 87 } #Rockies
							}
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }

					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_LBJ_ocean_dumping_act = {
		allowed = {
			tag = USA
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = USA_Muskie_movement
		}
		available = {
			tag = USA
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 40
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_LBJ_ocean_dumping_act"
			add_to_variable = { LBJ_environment_strength = 1 }
			USA_lbj_strengthen_enviroment_medium = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = LBJ_anger_coastal_states
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = { state = 366 state = 378 state = 371 state = 952 state = 949 state = 359 state = 358 state = 365 state = 357 state = 370 state = 954 state = 370 state = 361 state = 951 state = 375 state = 363 state = 385 state = 386 state = 362 state = 948 state = 367 }
					}
					set_state_flag = state_angry_ocean_dumping
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { RD_popularity < NPP_popularity}
							check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity < RD_D_bonus_popularity}
						}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05}
						add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = -0.05}
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
						add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = -0.05}
					}
					else = {
							add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05}
							add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = -0.05}
							add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
							add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = -0.05}
						}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
						NOT = { has_state_flag = state_angry_ocean_dumping }
					}
					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = -0.05}
					add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
					add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = -0.05}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes}
					clr_state_flag = state_angry_ocean_dumping
				}
			}
		}
	}

##################################################################

######### Response Tree mission

##################################################################

USA_react_to_last_potus = {
	respond_to_potus = {
		visible = {
			original_tag = USA
		}
		available = { #Mission is completed when the player finishes their response tree
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = USA_response_mission_requirement_tt
				has_country_flag = USA_finished_response
			}
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = USA_begin_response
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 180 #Undo the misstakes of the previous POTUS in 6 months or get screwed
		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = response_mission_fracture_party_tt
			add_stability = -0.07
			if = { #Check for what party is in charge and give their unity a severe blow
				limit = { #NPP
					OR = {
						has_government = social_democrat
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						has_government = national_socialism
						has_government = communist
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { USA_NPP_Unity = 5 }
			}
			else = { #RD
				subtract_from_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD_Past
					}
				}
				USA_response_anger_north = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_response_anger_north_tt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD_Past
					}
				}
				USA_response_anger_south = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_response_anger_south_tt
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { #Hooray you prevented the party from fracturing
			clr_country_flag = USA_begin_response
			hidden_effect = {
				USA_reload_presidential_tree = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

 USA_UAR_Humanitarian_category = {

	USA_Medicine_Drops_EGB = {
		visible = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Help_The_Refugees
			country_exists = EGB
		}
		available = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Help_The_Refugees
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { always = yes }
		cost = 150
		days_remove = 15
		days_re_enable = 15
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_Humanitarian_Airdrops_EGB"
			EGB = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment_1
					amount = 85
					producer = USA
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				USA = {
					add_to_variable = { misc_costs = 10 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_Engineers_EGB = {
		visible = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Help_The_Refugees
			country_exists = EGB
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_3 }
		}
		available = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Help_The_Refugees
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_3 }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { always = yes }
		cost = 200
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 90
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_Engineers_EGB"
			EGB = {
				add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				USA = {
					add_to_variable = { misc_costs = 50 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_1
						has_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_2
						has_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_3
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_1
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_1
				set_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_2
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_2
				set_country_flag = USA_Engineers_EGB_3
			}
		}
	}

	USA_Propaganda_Leaflets_EGB = {
		visible = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Help_The_Refugees
			country_exists = EGB
		}

	USA_Send_Mercs_EGB = {
		visible = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Spread_The_Cash
			country_exists = EGB
		}
		available = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Spread_The_Cash
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { always = yes }
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 90
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_Send_Mercs_EGB"
			EGB = {
				add_manpower = 1000
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				USA = {
					add_to_variable = { misc_costs = 10 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_Gunsmiths_EGB = {
		visible = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Spread_The_Cash
			country_exists = EGB
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_3 }
		}
		available = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Spread_The_Cash
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_3 }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { always = yes }
		cost = 200
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 90
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_Gunsmiths_EGB"
			EGB = {
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				USA = {
					add_to_variable = { misc_costs = 50 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_1
						has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_2
						has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_3
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_1
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_1
				set_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_2
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_2
				set_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_EGB_3
			}
		}
	}

	USA_Gunsmiths_OMB = {
		visible = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Spread_The_Cash
			country_exists = OMB
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_3 }
		}
		available = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_completed_focus = USA_Spread_The_Cash
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_3 }
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { always = yes }
		cost = 200
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 90
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_Gunsmiths_OMB"
			OMB = {
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				USA = {
					add_to_variable = { misc_costs = 50 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_1
						has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_2
						has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_3
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_1
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_1
				set_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_2
				}
				clr_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_2
				set_country_flag = USA_Gunsmiths_OMB_3
			}
		}
	}

USA_WAL_variables_category = {

	USA_wal_meet_with_Harrington = {
		visible = {}
		available = {}
		cost = 150
		fire_only_once = yes 

		ai_will_do = { #do only if the south is satisfied
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					check_variable = { wal_seg_minus_expect < 1 }
					check_variable = { wal_sr_minus_expect < 1 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_add_NPP_unity
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_Unity = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = wal_add_expectations_tt
			add_to_variable = { WAL_SEGREGATION_expectation = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { WAL_STATES_RIGHTS_expectation = 2 }
			wallace_update_var_display = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = wallace.627
					days = 3
				}
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_wal_meet_with_Harrington"
		}
	}

	USA_wal_huge_southern_rally = {
		visible = {}
		available = {}
		cost = 150
		fire_only_once = yes 

		ai_will_do = { #do only if the south is really pissed
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					check_variable = { wal_seg_minus_expect > -6 }
					check_variable = { wal_sr_minus_expect > -6 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_subtract_NPP_unity
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_NPP_Unity = 1.5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = wal_subtract_expectations_tt
			subtract_from_variable = { WAL_SEGREGATION_expectation = 2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { WAL_STATES_RIGHTS_expectation = 2 }
			wallace_update_var_display = yes
			country_event = {
				id = wallace.628
				days = 3
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_wal_huge_southern_rally"
		}
	}

	USA_wal_ease_northern_fears = {
		visible = {}
		available = {}
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 80

		ai_will_do = { #do only if the south is satisfied

				factor = 0

		cost = 10
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MCS_talk_to_center
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { mcs_change_influence_center = 0.01 }
				subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_right = 0.005 }
				subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_south = 0.01 }
				set_variable = { mcs_center_satisfaction_change = 0.1 }
				set_variable = { mcs_right_satisfaction_change = -0.05 }
				set_variable = { mcs_south_satisfaction_change = -0.1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { mcs_left_influence > 0.1 }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_left = 0.01 }
					set_variable = { mcs_left_satisfaction_change = 0.1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { mcs_fascist_influence > 0.1 }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { mcs_change_influence_fascist = 0.01 }
					set_variable = { mcs_fascist_satisfaction_change = -0.1 }
				}
				mcs_influence_calculation = yes
				mcs_unity_check = yes
			}
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = USA
			has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
		}
		available = {

			has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP

						can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity > NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
								check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity > RD_D_bonus_popularity }
							}
						}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.015 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.015 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								AND = {
									check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity > NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
									check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity < RD_D_bonus_popularity }
								}
								AND = {
									check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity < NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
									check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity > RD_D_bonus_popularity }
								}
							}
						}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.005 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.005 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
					}

						limit = {
							OR = {
								check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
								check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
							}
						}
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.015 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.02 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.015 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.02 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity > NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
								check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity > RD_D_bonus_popularity }
							}
						}
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.015 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.015 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								AND = {
									check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity > NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
									check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity < RD_D_bonus_popularity }
								}
								AND = {
									check_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity < NPP_FR_bonus_popularity }
									check_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity > RD_D_bonus_popularity }
								}
							}
						}
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.005 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.005 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
					}
					else = {
						add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
						add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01 }
						add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.005 }
						subtract_from_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.01 }
					}
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = 0.005
				}
				add_to_variable = { mcs_change_influence_center = -0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { mcs_change_influence_right = 0.005 }
				add_to_variable = { mcs_change_influence_south = 0.01 }
				set_variable = { mcs_center_satisfaction_change = -0.15 }
				set_variable = { mcs_right_satisfaction_change = 0.1 }
				set_variable = { mcs_south_satisfaction_change = 0.15 }
				mcs_influence_calculation = yes
				mcs_unity_check = yes
			}
		}
	}

USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgent_Decision_Catagory = {

	################################################# Vietnam Path amd IRAQ Path

	USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Vietnam_Increase_Arms_Aid = {

		visible = { 
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated 	
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out } 
		}

		available = {
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 749 }
		}

		cost = 20
		days_remove = 15
		days_re_enable = 25

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Increase_Investment_Medium
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Help_Mandates_Fight_Medium

			add_to_variable = { USA_SAF_WAR_Investment = 4 }

			if = { limit = { COG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				send_equipment = { equipment = infantry_equipment amount = 250 target = COG }

				COG = {
					add_to_variable = { OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability = 0.04 }
					}
			}

			if = { limit = { ANG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				send_equipment = { equipment = infantry_equipment amount = 250 target = ANG }
				ANG = { add_to_variable = { OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability = 0.04 } }
			}

			if = { limit = { MZB = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				send_equipment = { equipment = infantry_equipment amount = 250 target = MZB }
				MZB = { add_to_variable = { OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability = 0.04 } }
			}
		}
	}


	USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Iraq_Path_Propaganda_Campaign = {

		visible = { 
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated 	
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out } 
		}

		cost = 40
		days_remove = 15
		days_re_enable = 25

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Increase_Investment_Low
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Help_Mandates_stabilize_Low

			add_to_variable = { USA_SAF_WAR_Investment = 2 }

			if = { limit = { COG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				COG = {
					add_political_power = 50
					add_stability = 0.005
				}
			}

			if = { limit = { ANG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				ANG = {
					add_political_power = 50
					add_stability = 0.005
				}
			}

			if = { limit = { MZB = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				MZB = {
					add_political_power = 50
					add_stability = 0.005
				}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Vietnam_Send_In_Advisors  = {

		visible = { 
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated 	
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out }
		}

		available = {
			has_manpower > 9000
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Combating_Rebels }
		}

		cost = 30
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 30

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Increase_Investment_Large
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Help_Mandates_Fight_Large

			set_country_flag = { flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Combating_Rebels days = 20 value = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { USA_SAF_WAR_Investment = 6 }

			if = { limit = { COG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				COG = {
					add_manpower = 3000
					add_to_variable = { OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability = 0.06 }
				}
			}

			if = { limit = { ANG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
					ANG = {
						add_manpower = 3000
						add_to_variable = { OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability = 0.06 }
					}
			}

			if = { limit = { MZB = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				MZB = {
					add_manpower = 3000
					add_to_variable = { OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability = 0.06 }
				}
			}
		}

	}


	USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Iraq_Path_Protect_The_People_Tactics = {

		visible = { 
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated 	
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out } }

		available = {
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 224 }
			has_equipment = { support_equipment > 44 }
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 15
		days_re_enable = 25

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Increase_Investment_Low
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Help_Mandates_stabilize_Medium

			add_to_variable = { USA_SAF_WAR_Investment = 2 }

			if = { limit = { COG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }

				COG = {
					add_stability = 0.02
					add_war_support = 0.01
				}
				send_equipment = { equipment = infantry_equipment amount = 75 target = COG }
				send_equipment = { equipment = support_equipment amount = 15 target = COG }
			}

			if = { limit = { ANG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
			ANG = {
				add_stability = 0.02
				add_war_support = 0.01
			}
				send_equipment = { equipment = infantry_equipment amount = 75 target = COG }
				send_equipment = { equipment = support_equipment amount = 15 target = COG }
			}

			if = { limit = { MZB = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				MZB = {
					add_stability = 0.02
					add_war_support = 0.01
					}
				send_equipment = { equipment = infantry_equipment amount = 75 target = COG }
				send_equipment = { equipment = support_equipment amount = 15 target = COG }
			}
		}

	}

	USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Vietnam_Bring_Out_Napalm = {

		visible = { 
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated 	
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out } 
		}

		available = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Combating_Rebels }
		}

		cost = 30
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 80

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Increase_Investment_Large
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Help_Mandates_Fight_Large
			set_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_War_Crime_Napalm_Activated

			set_country_flag = { flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Combating_Rebels days = 20 value = 1 }

			add_to_variable = { USA_SAF_WAR_Investment = 6 }


			if = { limit = { COG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				COG = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Napalm days = 90  }
					add_to_variable = { OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability = 0.06 }
				}
			}

			if = { limit = { ANG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				ANG = {
				add_timed_idea = { idea = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Napalm days = 90  }
				add_to_variable = { OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability = 0.06 }
					}
			}

			if = { limit = { MZB = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				MZB = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Napalm days = 90  }
					add_to_variable = { OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability = 0.06 }
					}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Iraq_Path_Expand_Outreach_Programs = {

		visible = { 
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated 	
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out } 
		}

		cost = 75
		days_remove = 45
		days_re_enable = 20

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Increase_Investment_Medium
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Help_Mandates_stabilize_Medium

			add_to_variable = { USA_SAF_WAR_Investment = 3 }

			if = { limit = { COG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				COG = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Expand_Outreach days = 45 }
				}
			}

			if = { limit = { ANG = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				ANG = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Expand_Outreach days = 45 }
				}
			}

			if = { limit = { MZB = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat } }
				MZB = {

	USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Vietnam_Provide_Intelligence = {

		visible = { 
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated 	
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out }

		}

		days_remove = 5

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pull_Out_Decision_Tooltip
		}

		remove_effect = {

			ANG = {
				clamp_variable = {
					var = OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability
					min = 0
					max = 1
				}
			}

			COG = {
				clamp_variable = {
					var = OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability
					min = 0
					max = 1
				}
			}

			MZB = {
				clamp_variable = {
					var = OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability
					min = 0
					max = 1
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = USA.saf.debug.9 }
			hidden_effect = { USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulling_Out_Effect = yes  }

			hidden_effect = {
				COG = {
					country_event = {
						id = OFN_AFR_DECOL_COG.0
						days = 1
					}
				}
				MZB = {
					country_event = {
						id = OFN_AFR_DECOL_MZB.0
						days = 1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_cosmetic_tag = USA_CAR
						}
						country_event = {
							id = OFN_AFR_DECOL_COG.0
							days = 1
						}
						country_event = {
							id = OFN_AFR_DECOL_ANG.0
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
				ANG = {
					country_event = {
						id = OFN_AFR_DECOL_ANG.0
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

USA_OFN_membership_category = {
	OFN_open_negotiations_with = {
		visible = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = OFN_opposes_new_member
					has_country_flag = OFN_neutral_new_member
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = OFN_membership_costs_trigger
				OR = {
					check_variable = { political_power > FROM.OFN_convince_cost_political }
					check_variable = { money_reserves > FROM.OFN_convince_cost_money }
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = OFN_membership_negotiation_trigger
				NOT = { has_country_flag = OFN_currently_negotiating_with_someone }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision OFN_open_negotiations_with target: [From.GetName]"
			custom_effect_tooltip = OFN_membership_start_negotiations
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { USA_currently_negotiating_with = FROM.id }
				set_variable = { USA_current_political_cost = FROM.OFN_convince_cost_political }
				set_variable = { USA_current_money_cost = FROM.OFN_convince_cost_money }
				set_country_flag = OFN_currently_negotiating_with_someone
				country_event = { id = OFN.membership.100 }
			}
		}
	}
	OFN_admit_member = {
		allowed = { tag = USA }
		visible = { has_country_flag = USA_OFN_new_membership_application }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = OFN_membership_all_in_favor
				all_of_scopes = {
					array = global.OFN_members
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = OFN_supports_new_member
						is_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		complete_effect = {
			USA = { add_to_faction = OFN_candidate }
			add_to_array = {
				global.OFN_members = var:OFN_candidate
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { OFN_candidate = ENG.id } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = ENG_GF_WonEcw
					}
					ENG = { country_event = ENG_International_Mechanic.10 }
				}
				ULS = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_subject_of = ENG
						}
						add_ideas = OFN_Dependent_Member
						add_to_array = {
							global.OFN_members = ULS
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { OFN_candidate = BRT.id } has_country_flag = BRT_ofn_delaporte_membership }
				add_ideas = OFN_Independent_Member
				BRT = { country_event = { id = BRT.79 } }
				clr_country_flag = BRT_ofn_delaporte_membership
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { OFN_candidate = BRT.id } has_country_flag = BRT_ofn_mordrel_membership }
				add_ideas = OFN_Independent_Member
				BRT = { country_event = { id = BRT.79 } }
				clr_country_flag = BRT_ofn_mordrel_membership
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					check_variable = { OFN_candidate = IBR.id }  
				}
				IBR = { 
					add_ideas = OFN_Independent_Member
					country_event = { 
						id =  IBR.707 
					} 
				}
			}
			USA_OFN_clear_candidate_vote = yes
		}
	}
	OFN_addition_timeout = {
		allowed = { tag = USA }
		visible = { has_country_flag = USA_OFN_new_membership_application }
		available = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_OFN_new_membership_application } }
		activation = { has_country_flag = USA_OFN_new_membership_application }
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { OFN_candidate = BRT.id } has_country_flag = BRT_ofn_delaporte_membership }
				clr_country_flag = BRT_ofn_delaporte_membership
				BRT = { country_event = { id = BRT.80 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { OFN_candidate = BRT.id } has_country_flag = BRT_ofn_mordrel_membership }
				clr_country_flag = BRT_ofn_mordrel_membership
				BRT = { country_event = { id = BRT.80 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					check_variable = { OFN_candidate = IBR.id }  
				}
				IBR = { 
					country_event = { 
						id =  IBR.706 
					} 
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_can_grant_iberia_oobserver_status
			}
			USA_OFN_clear_candidate_vote = yes
		}
		complete_effect = { }
	}
	OFN_grant_observer_status_iberia = {
		allowed = { tag = USA }
		visible = { has_country_flag = USA_can_grant_iberia_oobserver_status }
		complete_effect = {
			IBR = { country_event = { id = IBR.711 } }
			clr_country_flag = USA_can_grant_iberia_oobserver_status
		}
	}
}
